29801, Neutrophil differential count, A white blood cell (WBC) count measures the number of white blood cells in your blood. A WBC differential determines the percentage of each type of white blood cell present in your blood. A differential can also detect immature white blood cells or any abnormalities both of which are signs of a potential problem., IMPC_HEM_029_001
29802, Neutrophil cell count, A white blood cell (WBC) count measures the number of white blood cells in your blood.
